 elahabaad hoicourt faisla sunaane ke saath talwaar dampatti ko doshi tehraane ke trial court ke faisle par behad sakht tippanee kii

 isi tippanee ke saath elahabaad hoicourt ke justise arvind kumaar mishra ne faisla padhanaa khatm kiya
 The Allahabad High Court, the judge who raised the question, is a special CBI judge
 laal hai

 Justice Mishra continued to speak strong words against the CBI judge
